
OAuthHandler(consumer_key, consumer_secret)
auth.set_access_token(access_token, access_token_secret)
api = tweepy.API(auth)
?
i=0
?
for tweet in tweepy.Cursor(api.search,q="#MissUniverse2015",count=100,\
                           lang="en",\
                           since_id=2015-06-12).items():
    i=i+1
    print tweet.created_at, tweet.text,i
